First, I will preprocess the claim and contexts to remove any stop words and punctuation, and convert all words to lowercase. I will also tokenize the text by splitting it into individual words.

I will then multiply the TF and IDF scores together to get the final TF-IDF score for each term in each context.

After calculating the TF-IDF scores for each term in each context, I will sum up the scores for each context to get a single score representing the relevance, informativeness, and likelihood of containing the answer to the claim.
